[30;1m1 | [0m[35m# Spglib test-suite[0m
[30;1m2 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m3 | [0m[35mThe main Spglib test-suite is a standalone CMake project that can be executed on a pre-installed Spg[0m
[30;1m4 | [0m[35mpart of the main Spglib project. On top of this, there are language-dependent test-suites, e.g. `pyt[0m
